###
# FROM is the actor ie the initiator of the diplomatic action
# ROOT is the recipient of the diplomatic action

greetings = {

	### HOSTILE GREETINGS

	# Hostile Generic 1
	01_HOSTILE_GREETING = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
				is_xenophile = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_same_species = FROM
				is_at_war_with = FROM
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = FROM
				is_domineering_to = FROM
				is_unfriendly_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	# Hostile Generic 2
	02_HOSTILE_GREETING = {

	# Hostile Xenophile - Killed Tiyanki
	27_HOSTILE_GREETING = {
		trigger = {
			is_xenophile = yes
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_pest_control" }
			OR = {
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = from
					modifier = opinion_killed_tiyanki_fleet_1
				}
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = from
					modifier = opinion_killed_tiyanki_fleet_2
				}
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = from
					modifier = opinion_killed_all_tiyanki_1
				}
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = from
					modifier = opinion_killed_all_tiyanki_2
				}
			}
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = FROM
				is_domineering_to = FROM
				is_unfriendly_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}

			NOR = {
				is_xenophile = yes

	# Watchful Regulators
	WR_ARROGANT_GREETING_01 = {
		weight = {
			weight = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
			has_ai_personality = awakened_fallen_empire_materialist
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
			OR = {

		}

			is_machine_empire = yes
			has_civic = civic_machine_assimilator
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = from }
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = from

	S_MECH_VASSAL_GREETING_01 = {
		weight = {
			weight = 19000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_machine_empire = yes
			has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			AND = {
				exists = overlord
				overlord = { is_same_value = FROM }
				NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
				NOT = { is_disloyal_to = FROM }
			}
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_species_class = ROBOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Organic to Mechanical Empire GREETINGS

	ORG_MECH_HOSTILE_GREETING_01 = {
		weight = {
			weight = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = from
				is_unfriendly_to = from
			}
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
				is_species_class = ROBOT
				is_spiritualist = yes
				is_egalitarian = yes
				is_at_war_with = FROM
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:ratling_country
					is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
				}
			}
			from = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ORG_MECH_HOSTILE_GREETING_02 = {
		weight = {
			weight = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = from
				is_unfriendly_to = from
			}
			NOR = {
				is_machine_empire = yes

				is_at_war_with = FROM
				AND = {
					exists = event_target:ratling_country
					is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
				}
			}
			from = {
				OR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					has_country_flag = synthetic_empire
					is_species_class = ROBOT
				}
			}
		}

	# Colossus Greetings
	FRIENDLY_COLOSSUS_GREETING_01 = {
		trigger = {
			any_controlled_ship = { is_ship_size = colossus }
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
				has_valid_civic = civic_fanatic_purifiers
				is_at_war_with = FROM
				is_pacifist = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_friendly_to = FROM
				is_cordial_to = FROM
				is_protective_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}

		weight = {
			weight = 100000
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = FROM
				is_domineering_to = FROM
				is_unfriendly_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}

				has_ai_personality = exterminators
			}
		}
		# Gen Machine Empire
		MECH_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_ACCEPT = {
			only_for_trade = yes
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				is_fallen_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		# Organics to Machines
		ORG_TO_MECH_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_ACCEPT_01 = {
			only_for_trade = yes
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						is_species_class = ROBOT
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				weight = 20
			}
		}
		# Ketlings
		KET_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_ACCEPT_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 100000 }
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
		# Corporate
		CORP_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_ACCEPT_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
		CORP_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_ACCEPT_02 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}
	refuse = {
		01_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_REFUSE_FE = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
			}
		}
		01_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_REFUSE_MACHINE_FE = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		01_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
			}
		}
		02_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {

					is_country_type = fallen_empire

				NOR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
			}
		}
		04_OFFER_TRADE_DEAL_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness

				}

		FALLEN_MACHINE_EMPIRE_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				is_fallen_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		01_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = event_target:ratling_country }
					AND = {
						exists = event_target:ratling_country
						NOT = { is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		HM_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind

				}
			}

			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = servitors
					has_ai_personality = assimilators
					has_ai_personality = exterminators
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_02 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = servitors
			}
		}
		A_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = assimilators
			}
		}
		MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {

			}
		}
		ORG_TO_MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes

			trigger = {

				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
		# Corporate
		CORP_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}

				}
				OR = {
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		02_MAKE_RIVAL_FRIENDLY = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness

					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM

			}
		}

action_integrate_subject = {
	select = {
		01_INTEGRATE_FRIENDLY = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
				}
				FROM = { NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes } }
			}
		}
		HM_INTEGRATE_FRIENDLY = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind
					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
				OR = {
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		# Gen Machine Empire
		MECH_INTEGRATE_FRIENDLY = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				OR = {
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		# Organics to Machines
		ORG_TO_MECH_INTEGRATE_FRIENDLY_01 = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				OR = {
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				weight = 20
			}
		}
		ORG_TO_MECH_INTEGRATE_NEUTRAL_01 = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_species_class = ROBOT
					is_friendly_to = FROM
					is_protective_to = FROM
					is_cordial_to = FROM
					is_hostile_to = FROM
					is_domineering_to = FROM
					is_unfriendly_to = FROM
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				weight = 20
			}
		}
		ORG_TO_MECH_INTEGRATE_HOSTILE_01 = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				OR = {
					is_hostile_to = FROM
					is_domineering_to = FROM
					is_unfriendly_to = FROM
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				weight = 20
			}
		}

		01_INTEGRATE_NEUTRAL = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				#OR = {
				#	is_neutral_to = FROM
				#	is_threatened_to = FROM
				#}
				NOT = { is_friendly_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_cordial_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_protective_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_hostile_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_domineering_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_unfriendly_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_dismissive_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_patronizing_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_angry_to = FROM }
			}
		}
		HM_INTEGRATE_NEUTRAL = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind

				}
				NOT = { is_friendly_to = FROM }
				NOT = { is_cordial_to = FROM }

		02_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_authority = auth_dictatorial
					has_authority = auth_imperial

action_support_independence = {
	select = {
		01_SUPPORT_INDEPENDENCE_SELECT_LOYAL = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_megacorp = yes
					is_species_class = ROBOT
					is_at_war_with = overlord
					is_disloyal_to = overlord
				}
			}
		}
		01_SUPPORT_INDEPENDENCE_SELECT_DISLOYAL = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_at_war_with = overlord
					is_disloyal_to = overlord

					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_at_war_with = overlord
					is_disloyal_to = overlord
				}
			}
		}
	}

	propose = {
		01_REVOKE_INDEPENDENCE_PROPOSE = {
			trigger = {
				from = {
					NOR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						is_megacorp = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	accept = {
		01_REVOKE_INDEPENDENCE_ACCEPT_LOYAL = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_megacorp = yes
					is_species_class = ROBOT
					is_at_war_with = overlord
					is_disloyal_to = overlord

action_form_migration_pact = {
	consider = {
		02_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_authority = auth_dictatorial
					has_authority = auth_imperial
					#has_government = military_dictatorship
					#has_government = martial_empire
					#has_government = divine_mandate
					#has_government = transcendent_empire
					#has_government = despotic_hegemony
					#has_government = ai_overlordship
					#has_government = enlightened_monarchy
					#has_government = irenic_monarchy
					#has_government = despotic_empire
					#has_government = star_empire
				}
			}
		}
		03_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_authority = auth_oligarchic
					#has_government = tec_military_council
					#has_government = ordered_stratocracy
					#has_government = theocratic_oligarchy
					#has_government = transcendent_oligarchy
					#has_government = science_directorate
					#has_government = illuminated_technocracy
					#has_government = peaceful_bureaucracy
					#has_government = irenic_protectorate
					#has_government = plutocratic_oligarchy
					#has_government = mega_corporation
				}
			}
		}
		04_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_authority = auth_democratic
					#has_government = military_republic
					#has_government = martial_demarchy
					#has_government = theocratic_republic
					#has_government = transcendent_republic
					#has_government = direct_democracy
					#has_government = subconscious_consensus
					#has_government = moral_democracy
					#has_government = irenic_democracy
					#has_government = indirect_democracy
					#has_government = democratic_utopia
				}
			}
		}
		HM_CONSIDER_02 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind
					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
			}
		}
		HM_CONSIDER_03 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind
					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
			}
		}
		HM_CONSIDER_04 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind
					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = servitors
					has_ai_personality = assimilators
					has_ai_personality = exterminators
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_02 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = servitors
			}
		}
		A_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = assimilators
			}
		}
		MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		ORG_TO_MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						is_species_class = ROBOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KET_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 100000 }
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
		# Corporate
		CORP_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}
	select = {
		01_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_SELECT = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = event_target:ratling_country }
					AND = {
						exists = event_target:ratling_country
						NOT = { is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country }
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_megacorp = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	propose = {
		01_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_PROPOSE = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						exists = event_target:ratling_country
						FROM = { NOT = { is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country } }
					}
					NOT = { exists = event_target:ratling_country }
				}
				NOT = { FROM = { is_megacorp = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	accept = {
		01_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_ACCEPT = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = event_target:ratling_country }
					AND = {
						exists = event_target:ratling_country
						NOT = { is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country }
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_megacorp = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	refuse = {
		01_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = event_target:ratling_country }
					AND = {
						exists = event_target:ratling_country
						NOT = { is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country }
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_megacorp = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	# Ketlings
	select = {
		KET_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_SELECT = {
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
	}
	propose = {
		KET_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_PROPOSE = {
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				FROM = {
					is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
				}
			}
		}
	}
	accept = {
		KET_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_ACCEPT = {
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
	}
	refuse = {
		KET_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
	}
	# Corporate
	select = {
		CORP_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_SELECT_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}
	propose = {
		CORP_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_PROPOSE_01 = {
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	accept = {
		CORP_FORM_MIGRATION_PACT_ACCEPT_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}

			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}

					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = servitors
					has_ai_personality = assimilators
					has_ai_personality = exterminators
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_02 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = servitors
			}
		}
		A_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = assimilators
			}
		}
		MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		ORG_TO_MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						is_species_class = ROBOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Ketlings
		KET_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 100000 }
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
		# Corporate
		CORP_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}
	select = {
		01_DEMAND_TRIBUTARY_SELECT = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_machine_empire = yes
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	propose = {
		01_DEMAND_TRIBUTARY_PROPOSE = {
			trigger = {
				from = {
					NOR = {
						is_machine_empire = yes
						is_megacorp = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	consider = {
		FALLEN_MACHINE_EMPIRE_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				is_fallen_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		01_CONSIDER = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
					is_megacorp = yes
				}
			}
		}
		HM_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = hive_mind
					has_ai_personality = devouring_swarm
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = servitors
					has_ai_personality = assimilators
					has_ai_personality = exterminators
				}
			}
		}
		S_CONSIDER_02 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality = servitors
				}
			}
		}
		A_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 50 }
			trigger = {
				has_ai_personality = assimilators
			}
		}
		MECH_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		# Ketlings
		KET_CONSIDER_01 = {
			weight = { weight = 100000 }
			trigger = {
				exists = event_target:ratling_country
				is_same_empire = event_target:ratling_country
			}
		}
		# Corporate
		CORP_CONSIDER_01 = {
			trigger = {
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}
	select = { 01_DEMAND_SATELLITE_SELECT = { trigger = { always = yes } } }
	propose = { 01_DEMAND_SATELLITE_PROPOSE = { trigger = { always = yes } } }
	accept = {
		01_DEMAND_SATELLITE_ACCEPT = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	refuse = {
		01_DEMAND_SATELLITE_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	accept = {
		MECH_DEMAND_SATELLITE_ACCEPT = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
	}
	refuse = {
		MECH_DEMAND_SATELLITE_REFUSE = {
			trigger = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
	}
